GT Equivalence Verification (PO32)

GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*exp(-Abs(v))*v - omega0**c1*x**c2
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.0907*v³ - 0.5945*v*exp(-|v|) - 2.9429*x³ + 0.5691*sin(t)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `v³` term
2. `v*exp(-|v|)` term
3. `x³` term
4. `sin(t)` term

Let me analyze each candidate:

### Candidate 1: `c0*x³ + c1*x² + c2*v + c3*v*x² + c4*x + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t)*cos(c8*t + c9)`
Missing `v³`, `v*exp(-|v|)`. Has polynomial terms in x and v, and `exp(c7*t)*cos(c8*t+c9)`. Setting c7=0 gives cos(c8*t+c9) which can match sin(t). But no v³ or v*exp(-|v|) terms. Cannot match.
**Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 2: `c0*x² + c1*x + c2*v*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*cos(c6*t + c7) + c8*x⁵`
Missing v³, v*exp(-|v|), x³. Has x⁵ instead of x³. Cannot match.
**Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 3: `c0*x² + c1*x + c2 + c3*x³ + c4*exp(c5*t)*cos(c6*t + c7)`
Missing v³, v*exp(-|v|). No v-dependence at all. Cannot match.
**Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 4: `c0*x/(c1 + c2*exp(c3*x)) + c4*x³ + c5*v + c6*exp(c7*t)*cos(c8*t + c9)`
Missing v³, v*exp(-|v|). Has only linear v. The x/(c1+c2*exp(c3*x)) term cannot produce v-dependent terms. Cannot match.
**Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 5: `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v*Max(0, c3 + |v|) + c4*exp(c5*t)*cos(c6*t + c7)`
Has x³ ✓. The `exp(c5*t)*cos(c6*t+c7)` with c5=0 gives cos(c6*t+c7) = sin(t) with appropriate constants ✓.
The term `c2*v*Max(0, c3 + |v|)`: If c3 ≥ 0, Max(0, c3+|v|) = c3+|v| always. Then c2*v*(c3+|v|) = c2*c3*v + c2*v*|v|.
But GT needs v³ and v*exp(-|v|). v*|v| = v²*sign(v) ≠ v³. Actually v*|v| = |v|*v = v*|v|. For v>0: v*|v| = v², for v<0: v*|v| = -v². This is NOT v³ (which is v³ for v>0 and -v³ for v<0... wait, v³ for v<0 is negative cube). Actually v*|v| ≠ v³ since |v|≠v² and v*|v| = sign(v)*v² while v³ = v*v². These are different: v*|v| = |v|*v while v³ = v*v*v. For v>0: v*|v|=v², v³=v³. Different.
Also missing v*exp(-|v|). Cannot match.
**Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 6: `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*exp(c3*t)*cos(c4*t + c5)`
No v-dependence. Cannot match.
**Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 33: `c0*x² + c1*x + c2 + c3*v³ + c4*exp(c5*cos(c6*t)) + c7*x*|x|`
Note x*|x| = x³ for... wait, no. x*|x| = |x|*x = x²*sign(x). For x>0: x², for x<0: -x². But x³ for x>0 is x³, for x<0 is -|x|³. These are different. Actually wait: x*|x| gives sign(x)*x² while x³ = x*x². Hmm, x*|x| = sign(x)*x² and x³ = x*x*x. For x=2: x*|x|=4, x³=8. Different. So x*|x| ≠ x³.
